Toss until lightly coated, and arrange them in a single layer.","url":"https://cookieandkate.com/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice/#instruction-step-3"},{"@type":"HowToStep","text":"Roast the sweet potatoes on the middle rack for about 35 minutes, tossing halfway, and roast the peppers on the top rack for about 20 minutes, tossing halfway. The vegetables will be tender and caramelized on the edges when they are ready.","url":"https://cookieandkate.com/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice/#instruction-step-4"},{"@type":"HowToStep","text":"In the meantime, cook the rice: Once the water is boiling, pour in the rice and give it a stir. Boil the rice for 30 minutes, then turn off the heat and drain the rice. Return the rice to the pot and cover the pot. Let the rice steam that way for 10 minutes. Remove the lid, fluff the rice with a fork and season with salt to taste.","url":"https://cookieandkate.com/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice/#instruction-step-5"},{"@type":"HowToStep","text":"Make the sauce: In a bowl, whisk together the sauce ingredients. </header><div class="entry-content"><p class="entry-meta"><span class="entry-comments-link"><a href="https://cookieandkate.com/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice/#comments">280 Comments</a></span> </p><style style="display: none !important;">
.tasty-recipes-quick-links { text-align:center; }
.tasty-recipes-quick-links a { padding: 0.5rem; }
</style>
<div class="tasty-recipes-quick-links">
<a class="tasty-recipes-jump-link" href="#tasty-recipes-23466-jump-target">Jump to Recipe</a>
</div>
<p><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" class="aligncenter wp-image-31438 size-full" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201100%201650'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" width="1100" height="1650" data-lazy-srcset="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-4.jpg 1100w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-4-550x824.jpg 550w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-4-270x405.jpg 270w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-4-768x1152.jpg 768w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 480px) 90vw, (max-width: 865px) 80vw, 550px" data-lazy-src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-4.jpg" /><noscript><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" class="aligncenter wp-image-31438 size-full" src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-4.jpg" alt="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" width="1100" height="1650" srcset="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-4.jpg 1100w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-4-550x824.jpg 550w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-4-270x405.jpg 270w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-4-768x1152.jpg 768w" sizes="(max-width: 480px) 90vw, (max-width: 865px) 80vw, 550px" /></noscript></p>
<p>Please tell me that I am not the only girl who leaves her keys in the door. Or loses her car in parking lots. Or drops her wallet on the sidewalk. Distracted is my middle name, but committing all three of those mistakes over the past few weeks is a personal record.</p>
<p><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" data-pin-nopin="nopin" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-9149" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20550%20378'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="sweet potatoes" width="550" height="378" data-lazy-src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2013/10/sweet-potatoes.jpg" /><noscript><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" data-pin-nopin="nopin" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-9149" src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2013/10/sweet-potatoes.jpg" alt="sweet potatoes" width="550" height="378" /></noscript></p>
<p>I suppose I have to tell you the stories now, don&#8217;t I? I&#8217;ll start with the best one. A couple of weeks ago, I took Cookie outside before dragging myself to bed. I was exhausted—apparently so exhausted that I left my keys in my door when I shut it behind me. Dumb, right? The next morning, I woke up and searched around for my keys. I couldn&#8217;t find them in any of the normal spots. It finally occurred to me to check the door. Aha! Keys. Relief.</p>
<p>Then I walked down the front steps, looked over to my left, and saw my car. My car was parked in front of the fire hydrant with a white ticket flapping underneath the window wiper. <em>That&#8217;s not where I parked my car, you guys.</em> I walked over to my car with trepidation and peered through the windows.</p>
<p>Everything inside my car seemed to be in order. I got in and noticed that the seat had been scooted back a few inches. All I know about the thief (borrower?) is that he&#8217;s a few inches taller than me, drives a manual transmission and has an iPhone, apparently, since he took my cord with him. That leaves a lot of suspects.</p>
<p><span id="more-9141"></span><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" data-pin-nopin="nopin" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-9148" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20550%20378'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="red bell pepper and peanut butter" width="550" height="378" data-lazy-src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2013/10/red-bell-pepper-and-peanut-butter.jpg" /><noscript><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" data-pin-nopin="nopin" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-9148" src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2013/10/red-bell-pepper-and-peanut-butter.jpg" alt="red bell pepper and peanut butter" width="550" height="378" /></noscript></p>
<p>I&#8217;m still wondering what that stranger did in my car. Maybe he just wanted to cruise around the neighborhood. Maybe he ran out of beer and decided to drive over to the gas station. Maybe he intended to steal it, but quickly realized that stealing my beat-up car was a waste of time and brought it back. Maybe he dropped off some drugs. Let&#8217;s hope not. I just wish he&#8217;d dropped off the stuff in my trunk at Goodwill while he was at it.</p>
<p>The other stories aren&#8217;t so exciting. I was thirty minutes late to <a href="http://bevcooks.com" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Bev</a>&#8216;s baby shower (<a href="http://bevcooks.com/tag/pregnancy/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">she&#8217;s having twins!</a>) because I lost my car on The Plaza. Then my wallet fell out of my grandmother&#8217;s little black purse in between Sur la Table and the corner. Thankfully, a good samaritan found the wallet and brought it to customer service, which is what I would have done for him. All said and done, I&#8217;ve really lucked out in all of these situations. I have a sixty dollar ticket to pay but that&#8217;s not the worst that could have happened.</p>
<p><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" data-pin-nopin="nopin" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-9146" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20550%20378'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="green onions" width="550" height="378" data-lazy-src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2013/10/green-onions.jpg" /><noscript><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" data-pin-nopin="nopin" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-9146" src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2013/10/green-onions.jpg" alt="green onions" width="550" height="378" /></noscript></p>
<p>Sometimes I wish I had someone around to catch my silly mistakes in real time. I make a lot of them. I do have you all, though. You let me know when I list garlic twice in a recipe, or when there&#8217;s a little too much pumpkin in my pancakes. You leave feedback for me in the comments section and tweet/instagram/email me photos of the recipes you&#8217;ve made at home, which makes me super happy. Even if I don&#8217;t respond right away, know that I&#8217;m listening and glad you&#8217;re here.</p>
<p>This recipe, for example, was inspired by a convincing comment left on <a href="https://cookieandkate.com/baked-sweet-potato-fries/">my sweet potato fries recipe</a>. Carla said, &#8220;These are wonderful and are even more unbelievable with THAI SPICY PEANUT SAUCE. Sorry to yell, but these two things were born for each other. Ketchup, honey, mayo based sauces do not do them justice.&#8221;</p>
<p>She sounded like she was onto something, so I grabbed a bottle of <a href="http://www.san-j.com/product_info.asp?id=6" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">San-J Thai peanut sauce</a> at the store and roasted up some sweet potato fries. She was indeed onto something. I did my best to recreate San-J&#8217;s version based on the ingredient list. I switched from fries to <a href="https://cookieandkate.com/roasted-sweet-potatoes-recipe/">roasted sweet potatoes</a> and made it a full meal by adding jasmine rice, red bell pepper, cilantro and chives. Thanks, Carla!</p>
<p><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" class="aligncenter wp-image-31440 size-full" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201100%20800'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="roasted red bell pepper" width="1100" height="800" data-lazy-srcset="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-1.jpg 1100w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-1-550x400.jpg 550w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-1-270x196.jpg 270w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-1-768x559.jpg 768w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 480px) 90vw, (max-width: 865px) 80vw, 550px" data-lazy-src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-1.jpg" /><noscript><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" class="aligncenter wp-image-31440 size-full" src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-1.jpg" alt="roasted red bell pepper" width="1100" height="800" srcset="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-1.jpg 1100w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-1-550x400.jpg 550w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-1-270x196.jpg 270w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-1-768x559.jpg 768w" sizes="(max-width: 480px) 90vw, (max-width: 865px) 80vw, 550px" /></noscript></p>
<p><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" class="aligncenter wp-image-31441 size-full" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201099%20800'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Spicy Thai peanut sauce recipe" width="1099" height="800" data-lazy-srcset="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-2.jpg 1099w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-2-550x400.jpg 550w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-2-270x197.jpg 270w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-2-768x559.jpg 768w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 480px) 90vw, (max-width: 865px) 80vw, 550px" data-lazy-src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-2.jpg" /><noscript><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" class="aligncenter wp-image-31441 size-full" src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-2.jpg" alt="Spicy Thai peanut sauce recipe" width="1099" height="800" srcset="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-2.jpg 1099w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-2-550x400.jpg 550w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-2-270x197.jpg 270w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-2-768x559.jpg 768w" sizes="(max-width: 480px) 90vw, (max-width: 865px) 80vw, 550px" /></noscript></p>
<p><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" class="aligncenter wp-image-31439 size-full" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%201100%201643'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Roasted sweet potatoes with spicy Thai peanut sauce recipe" width="1100" height="1643" data-lazy-srcset="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-3.jpg 1100w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-3-550x822.jpg 550w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-3-270x403.jpg 270w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-3-768x1147.jpg 768w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 480px) 90vw, (max-width: 865px) 80vw, 550px" data-lazy-src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-3.jpg" /><noscript><img data-pin-title="Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice" class="aligncenter wp-image-31439 size-full" src="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-3.jpg" alt="Roasted sweet potatoes with spicy Thai peanut sauce recipe" width="1100" height="1643" srcset="https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-3.jpg 1100w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-3-550x822.jpg 550w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-3-270x403.jpg 270w, https://cookieandkate.com/images/2018/10/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice-3-768x1147.jpg 768w" sizes="(max-width: 480px) 90vw, (max-width: 865px) 80vw, 550px" /></noscript></p>

<h2>Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce over Roasted Sweet Potatoes and Rice</h2>
<div class="tasty-recipes-buttons">
<div class="tasty-recipes-button-wrap"><a class="button tasty-recipes-print-button tasty-recipes-no-print" href="https://cookieandkate.com/spicy-thai-peanut-sauce-over-roasted-sweet-potatoes-and-rice/print/23466/">Print</a></div>
<div id="save" data-relish-action="save" data-relish-save-toggle="true" data-relish-save-tab="none" class="button relish">save</div>
</div>
<div class="tasty-recipes-details">
<ul>
<li><span class="tasty-recipes-label">Author:</span> <span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-author-name">Cookie and Kate</span></li>
<li><span class="tasty-recipes-label">Prep Time:</span> <span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-prep-time">10 mins</span></li>
<li><span class="tasty-recipes-label">Cook Time:</span> <span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-cook-time">40 mins</span></li>
<li><span class="tasty-recipes-label">Total Time:</span> <span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-total-time">50 minutes</span></li>
<li><span class="tasty-recipes-label">Yield:</span> <span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-yield"><span data-amount="4">4</span> <span class="tasty-recipes-yield-scale"><span data-amount="1">1</span>x</span></span></li>
<li><span class="tasty-recipes-label">Category:</span> <span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-category">Main</span></li>
<li><span class="tasty-recipes-label">Cuisine:</span> <span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-cuisine">Thai</span></li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="tasty-recipes-ratings">
<div class="tasty-recipes-ratings-inner">
<p><span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-rating tasty-recipes-clip-100 tasty-recipes-rating-solid">&#9733;</span><span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-rating tasty-recipes-clip-100 tasty-recipes-rating-solid">&#9733;</span><span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-rating tasty-recipes-clip-100 tasty-recipes-rating-solid">&#9733;</span><span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-rating tasty-recipes-clip-100 tasty-recipes-rating-solid">&#9733;</span><span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-value-color.color" class="tasty-recipes-rating tasty-recipes-clip-90 tasty-recipes-rating-solid">&#9733;</span></p>
<p><span data-tasty-recipes-customization="detail-label-color.color" class="rating-label"><span class="average">4.9</span> from <span class="count">99</span> reviews</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="tasty-recipes-description">
<p>Bold and spicy Thai peanut sauce drizzled over roasted sweet potatoes and bell peppers on a bed of rice. The sauce would also be great on stir-fries and salads, or as a dip for raw vegetables. This is a healthy vegetarian, vegan and gluten-free recipe.</p>
</div>
<div class="tasty-recipe-ingredients">
<span class="tasty-recipes-scale-container">
<span class="tasty-recipes-scale-label">Scale</span>
<button class="tasty-recipes-scale-button tasty-recipes-scale-button-active" data-amount="1" type="button">1x</button><button class="tasty-recipes-scale-button" data-amount="2" type="button">2x</button><button class="tasty-recipes-scale-button" data-amount="3" type="button">3x</button> </span>
<h3>Ingredients</h3>
<h4>Spicy Thai Peanut Sauce</h4>
<ul>
<li><span data-amount="0.5" data-unit="cup">&frac12; cup</span> creamy peanut butter</li>
<li><span data-amount="0.25" data-unit="cup">&frac14; cup</span> reduced-sodium tamari or soy sauce</li>
<li><span data-amount="3" data-unit="tablespoon">3 tablespoons</span> apple cider vinegar</li>
<li><span data-amount="2" data-unit="tablespoon">2 tablespoons</span> honey or maple syrup</li>
<li><span data-amount="1" data-unit="teaspoon">1 teaspoon</span> grated fresh ginger</li>
<li><span data-amount="2">2</span> cloves garlic, pressed</li>
<li><span data-amount="0.25" data-unit="teaspoon">&frac14; teaspoon</span> red pepper flakes</li>
<li><span data-amount="2" data-unit="tablespoon">2 tablespoons</span> water</li>
</ul>
<h4>Roasted vegetables</h4>
<ul>
<li><span data-amount="2">2</span> sweet potatoes, peeled and sliced into <span data-amount="1">1</span> inch long, &frac12; inch wide chunks</li>
<li><span data-amount="1">1</span> red bell pepper, cored, deseeded, and sliced into bite-sized strips</li>
<li>about <span data-amount="2" data-unit="tablespoon">2 tablespoons</span> coconut oil (or olive oil)</li>
<li><span data-amount="0.25" data-unit="teaspoon">&frac14; teaspoon</span> cumin powder</li>
<li>Sea salt, to taste</li>
</ul>
<h4>Rice and garnishes</h4>
<ul>
<li><span data-amount="1.25" data-unit="cup">1 &frac14; cup</span> jasmine brown rice (or any variety of long-grain brown rice)</li>
<li><span data-amount="2">2</span> to <span data-amount="3">3</span> green onions/chives, sliced into thin rounds (green and white parts)</li>
<li>Handful cilantro, torn</li>
<li>Handful peanuts, crushed</li>
<li>Sriracha/rooster sauce on the side (optional)</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="tasty-recipe-instructions">
<h3>Instructions</h3>
<ol>
<li id="instruction-step-1">Prep: Bring a large pot of water to boil. Preheat the oven to 425 degrees Fahrenheit with a rack in the middle and another rack near the top.</li>
<li id="instruction-step-2">Roast the vegetables: On a large, rimmed baking sheet, toss the sweet potato with a generous tablespoon of coconut oil, the cumin and a sprinkle of salt. Arrange them in a single layer, and set aside.</li>
<li id="instruction-step-3">On a separate, smaller baking sheet, toss the bell pepper with about 1 teaspoon of coconut oil and a sprinkle of salt. Toss until lightly coated, and arrange them in a single layer.</li>
<li id="instruction-step-4">Roast the sweet potatoes on the middle rack for about 35 minutes, tossing halfway, and roast the peppers on the top rack for about 20 minutes, tossing halfway. The vegetables will be tender and caramelized on the edges when they are ready.</li>
<li id="instruction-step-5">In the meantime, cook the rice: Once the water is boiling, pour in the rice and give it a stir. Boil the rice for 30 minutes, then turn off the heat and drain the rice. Return the rice to the pot and cover the pot. Let the rice steam that way for 10 minutes. Remove the lid, fluff the rice with a fork and season with salt to taste.</li>
<li id="instruction-step-6">Make the sauce: In a bowl, whisk together the sauce ingredients. If the sauce is too thick or too spicy, whisk in a little more water.</li>
<li id="instruction-step-7">Serve: In bowls, divide the rice and roasted vegetables. Drizzle each bowl generously with sauce, and top with a sprinkle of green onions, cilantro and peanuts.</li>
</ol>
</div>
<div class="tasty-recipes-notes">
<h3>Notes</h3>
<p><strong>Storage suggestions:</strong> Leftover sauce should keep well, refrigerated and covered, for a couple of weeks. Wake up the flavors with a little bit of apple cider vinegar or tamari if necessary.</p>
<p><strong>Make it gluten free:</strong> Tamari is a Japanese soy sauce that has a great flavor and is gluten free, unlike most other soy sauces. I like the San-J brand.<br />
<strong>Make it vegan:</strong> Use maple syrup instead of honey for vegan sauce.<br />
<strong>Other recipes you might like:</strong> my <a href="https://cookieandkate.com/2012/summer-rolls-with-spicy-peanut-sauce/">summer rolls with spicy peanut sauce</a>, <a href="https://cookieandkate.com/2011/peanut-soba-noodle-bowl/">peanut soba noodle bowl</a> and <a href="https://cookieandkate.com/2012/vegetarian-thai-green-curry/">Thai green curry</a>. Jeanine is also on a peanut sauce kick with <a href="http://www.loveandlemons.com/2013/10/06/easy-peanut-noodles/">peanut noodles and salad wraps</a>.</p>
</div>

		return ret === 2;
	};
	var frac =function frac(x,D,mixed){var n1=Math.floor(x),d1=1;var n2=n1+1,d2=1;if(x!==n1)while(bothEquals(d1,d2,D)){var m=(n1+n2)/(d1+d2);if(x===m){if(d1+d2<=D){d1+=d2;n1+=n2;d2=D+1}else if(d1>d2)d2=D+1;else d1=D+1;break}else if(x<m){n2=n1+n2;d2=d1+d2}else{n1=n1+n2;d1=d1+d2}}if(d1>D){d1=d2;n1=n2}if(!mixed)return[0,n1,d1];var q=Math.floor(n1/d1);return[q,n1-q*d1,d1]};frac.cont=function cont(x,D,mixed){var sgn=x<0?-1:1;var B=x*sgn;var P_2=0,P_1=1,P=0;var Q_2=1,Q_1=0,Q=0;var A=Math.floor(B);while(Q_1<D){A=Math.floor(B);P=A*P_1+P_2;Q=A*Q_1+Q_2;if(B-A<5e-8)break;B=1/(B-A);P_2=P_1;P_1=P;Q_2=Q_1;Q_1=Q}if(Q>D){if(Q_1>D){Q=Q_2;P=P_2}else{Q=Q_1;P=P_1}}if(!mixed)return[0,sgn*P,Q];var q=Math.floor(sgn*P/Q);return[q,sgn*P-q*Q,Q]};

	/* {'¼': '&frac14;','½': '&frac12;','¾': '&frac34;','⅓': '&#8531;','⅔':'&#8532;','⅕':'&#8533;','⅖':'2/5','⅗':'3/5','⅘':'&#8536;','⅙':'&#8537;','⅚':'&#8538;','⅛':'&#8539;','⅜':'&#8540;','⅝':'&#8541;','⅞':'&#8542;'} */
	window.tastyRecipesVulgarFractions = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent("%7B%22%C2%BC%22%3A%221%2F4%22%2C%22%C2%BD%22%3A%221%2F2%22%2C%22%C2%BE%22%3A%223%2F4%22%2C%22%E2%85%93%22%3A%221%2F3%22%2C%22%E2%85%94%22%3A%222%2F3%22%2C%22%E2%85%95%22%3A%221%2F5%22%2C%22%E2%85%96%22%3A%222%2F5%22%2C%22%E2%85%97%22%3A%223%2F5%22%2C%22%E2%85%98%22%3A%224%2F5%22%2C%22%E2%85%99%22%3A%221%2F6%22%2C%22%E2%85%9A%22%3A%225%2F6%22%2C%22%E2%85%9B%22%3A%221%2F8%22%2C%22%E2%85%9C%22%3A%223%2F8%22%2C%22%E2%85%9D%22%3A%225%2F8%22%2C%22%E2%85%9E%22%3A%227%2F8%22%7D"));

	window.tastyRecipesFormatAmount = function(amount, el) {
		if ( parseFloat( amount ) === parseInt( amount ) ) {
			return amount;
		}
		var roundType = 'frac';
		if (typeof el.dataset.amountShouldRound !== 'undefined') {
			if ('false' != el.dataset.amountShouldRound) {
				if ( 'number' === el.dataset.amountShouldRound ) {
					roundType = 'number';
				} else if ('frac' === el.dataset.amountShouldRound) {
					roundType = 'frac'
				} else if ('vulgar' === el.dataset.amountShouldRound) {
					roundType = 'vulgar'
				} else {
					roundType = 'integer';
				}
			}
		}
		if ('number' === roundType) {
			amount = Number.parseFloat(amount).toPrecision(2);
		} else if ('integer' === roundType) {
			amount = Math.round(amount);
		} else if ('frac' === roundType || 'vulgar' === roundType) {
			var denom = 8;
			if (typeof el.dataset.unit !== 'undefined') {
				var unit = el.dataset.unit;
				if (['cups','cup','c'].includes(unit)) {
					denom = 4;
					if (0.125 === amount) {
						denom = 8;
					}
					if ("0.1667" === Number.parseFloat( amount ).toPrecision(4)) {
						denom = 6;
					}
				}
				if (['tablespoons','tablespoon','tbsp'].includes(unit)) {
					denom = 2;
				}
				if (['teaspoons','teaspoon','tsp'].includes(unit)) {
					denom = 8;
				}
			}
			var amountArray = frac.cont( amount, denom, true );
			var newAmount = '';
			if ( amountArray[1] !== 0 ) {
				newAmount = amountArray[1] + '/' + amountArray[2];
				if ('vulgar' === roundType) {
					Object.keys(window.tastyRecipesVulgarFractions).forEach(function(vulgar) {
						if (newAmount === window.tastyRecipesVulgarFractions[vulgar]) {
							newAmount = vulgar;
						}
					});
				}
			}
			if ( newAmount ) {
				newAmount = ' ' + newAmount;
			}
			if ( amountArray[0] ) {
				newAmount = amountArray[0] + newAmount;
			}
			amount = newAmount;
		}
		return amount;
	}
}())

</script>
<script type="text/javascript" style="display: none !important;">
(function(){
	var buttonClass = 'tasty-recipes-scale-button',
		buttonActiveClass = 'tasty-recipes-scale-button-active',
		buttons = document.querySelectorAll('.tasty-recipes-scale-button');
	if ( ! buttons ) {
		return;
	}

	buttons.forEach(function(button){
		button.addEventListener('click', function(event){
			event.preventDefault();
			var recipe = event.target.closest('.tasty-recipes');
			if ( ! recipe ) {
				return;
			}
			var otherButtons = recipe.querySelectorAll('.' + buttonClass);
			otherButtons.forEach(function(bt){
				bt.classList.remove(buttonActiveClass);
			});
			button.classList.add(buttonActiveClass);

			/* Scales all scalable amounts. */
			var scalables = recipe.querySelectorAll('span[data-amount]');
			var buttonAmount = parseFloat( button.dataset.amount );
			scalables.forEach(function(scalable){
				if (typeof scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType === 'undefined'
					&& typeof scalable.dataset.nfOriginal === 'undefined') {
					if (-1 !== scalable.innerText.indexOf('/')) {
						scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType = 'frac';
					}
					if (-1 !== scalable.innerText.indexOf('.')) {
						scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType = 'number';
					}
					Object.keys(window.tastyRecipesVulgarFractions).forEach(function(vulgar) {
						if (-1 !== scalable.innerText.indexOf(vulgar)) {
							scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType = 'vulgar';
						}
					})
					if (typeof scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType !== 'undefined') {
						scalable.dataset.amountShouldRound = scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType;
					}
				}
				var amount = parseFloat( scalable.dataset.amount ) * buttonAmount;
				amount = window.tastyRecipesFormatAmount(amount, scalable);
				if ( typeof scalable.dataset.unit !== 'undefined' ) {
					if ( ! scalable.classList.contains('nutrifox-quantity') ) {
						if ( ! scalable.classList.contains('nutrifox-second-quantity') ) {
							amount += ' ' + scalable.dataset.unit;
						}
					}
				}
				scalable.innerText = amount;
			});
			/* Appends " (x2)" indicator. */
			var nonNumerics = recipe.querySelectorAll('[data-has-non-numeric-amount]');
			nonNumerics.forEach(function(nonNumeric){
				var indicator = nonNumeric.querySelector('span[data-non-numeric-label]');
				if ( indicator ) {
					nonNumeric.removeChild(indicator);
				}
				if ( 1 !== buttonAmount ) {
					var indicator = document.createElement('span');
					indicator.setAttribute('data-non-numeric-label', true);
					var text = document.createTextNode(' (x' + buttonAmount + ')');
					indicator.appendChild(text);
					nonNumeric.appendChild(indicator);
				}
			});
		});
	});
}());

</script></div>

<li class="comment even thread-even depth-1" id="comment-488576">

<header class="comment-header">
<p class="comment-author">
<span class="comment-author-name">Helen Sweeney</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time">September 5, 2018</time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>I&#8217;ve made this recipe a few times now, most recently for friends last night. Always a hit!</p>

<span class="comment-author-name">Eva Ellison</span> </p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time">January 25, 2019</time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>Second Cookie &amp; Kate recipe this week. I wasn&#8217;t 100% sure about the combo, but I love all the ingredients, especially savory peanut butter (yet can&#8217;t stand sweet lol).<br />
This turned out AMAZING! I didn&#8217;t add the red pepper flakes because any time I use them on a family meal, the kiddos refuse to eat it. Instead I used some Asian chili garlic sauce to give it a hint of heat.<br />
The potatoes were great the peppers were great, the sauce was great. I started my rice in the instant pot when I put my potatoes in and it was all done at the same time. It was the perfect balance of sweet &amp; savory.<br />
The kids both loved this dinner and I&#8217;ll definitely be making it again.</p>

<p>This is my family’s favorite recipe! It’s so good with all types of rice, and is the best! The sauce is so creamy and the perfect amount of spicy and the roasted veggies are the yummiest!</p>

						if (jQuery(evt.target).closest('#siq-menu-searchbox-wrap').length || jQuery(evt.target).closest('.siq-icon-searchbox-wrap').length)
							return;

						if (searchBox.hasClass('siq-search-open')) {
							searchBox.removeClass('siq-search-open');
						}
					});
				});
			}
		</script>
